--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ar/ArConstants.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar

object ARConstants {
    // Standard 8-foot table dimensions in meters (playing surface)
    const val TABLE_WIDTH = 1.12f  // 44 inches
    const val TABLE_DEPTH = 2.24f // 88 inches
    const val BALL_DIAMETER = 0.05715f

    // Dimensions for rendering the table rails
    const val RAIL_HEIGHT = 0.04f
    const val RAIL_WIDTH = 0.07f // A bit wider for a substantial look
}


--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ar/ArViewRenderer.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar

import android.content.Context
import androidx.compose.ui.geometry.Offset
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar.MathUtils.angleBetween
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar.MathUtils.normalize
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar.MathUtils.toF3
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui.Rail
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui.theme.AccentGold
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui.theme.RustedEmber
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui.theme.WarningRed
import dev.romainguy.kotlin.math.Float3
import dev.romainguy.kotlin.math.Quaternion
import dev.romainguy.kotlin.math.inverse
import io.github.sceneview.ar.node.AnchorNode
import io.github.sceneview.math.Position
import io.github.sceneview.math.Rotation
import io.github.sceneview.math.toNewQuaternion
import io.github.sceneview.math.toNewVector3
import io.github.sceneview.node.Node
import kotlinx.coroutines.CoroutineScope
import androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color
import io.github.sceneview.math.toOldQuaternion
import io.github.sceneview.utils.lookAt

object ARViewRenderer {

    private const val MAX_SQUIRT_DEGREES = 2.5f
    private const val MAX_THROW_DEGREES = 3.0f

    fun drawCutShotLines(anchorNode: AnchorNode, scope: CoroutineScope, context: Context, cuePos: Position, objPos: Position, spinOffset: Offset) {
        val cueF3 = cuePos.toF3()
        val objF3 = objPos.toF3()

        // Calculate squirt (cue ball deflection)
        val squirtAngle = -spinOffset.x * MAX_SQUIRT_DEGREES
        val squirtRotation = Quaternion.fromAxisAngle(Float3(y = 1f), squirtAngle)
        val initialAimVector = (objF3 - cueF3).normalize()
        val deflectedAimVector = squirtRotation * initialAimVector

        // Ghost ball based on original aim, not deflected aim
        val directionToObj = (cueF3 - objF3).normalize()
        val ghostBallPos = objF3 + directionToObj * ARConstants.BALL_DIAMETER
        anchorNode.addChild(BallNode(scope, Color.White.copy(alpha = 0.5f)).apply { position = ghostBallPos })

        // 1. Deflected Shot Line & Cue Stick
        val shotLineEnd = cueF3 + deflectedAimVector * 3f
        anchorNode.addChild(LineNode(scope, cueF3, shotLineEnd, AccentGold.copy(alpha = 0.7f), radius = 0.003f))
        val cueStickStart = cueF3 - deflectedAimVector * 1.5f
        anchorNode.addChild(LineNode(scope, cueStickStart, cueF3, Color.Gray, radius = 0.005f))


        // 2. Calculate throw (object ball deflection)
        val throwAngle = -spinOffset.x * MAX_THROW_DEGREES
        val throwRotation = Quaternion.fromAxisAngle(Float3(y = 1f), throwAngle)
        val initialObjTrajectory = (objF3 - ghostBallPos).normalize()
        val thrownObjTrajectory = throwRotation * initialObjTrajectory
        val objTrajectoryEnd = objF3 + thrownObjTrajectory * 3f
        anchorNode.addChild(LineNode(scope, objF3, objTrajectoryEnd, RustedEmber))


        // 3. Angle Text
        val cutAngle = angleBetween(shotLineEnd - cueF3, objTrajectoryEnd - objF3)
        val angleText = "%.1f°".format(cutAngle)
        val textPosition = objPos + Position(y = 0.1f)
        anchorNode.addChild(TextNode(scope, context, angleText))
            .apply { position = textPosition }
    }

    fun drawBankShotLines(
        anchorNode: AnchorNode,
        scope: CoroutineScope,
        context: Context,
        cuePos: Position,
        objPos: Position,
        selectedRail: Rail
    ) {
        val cueF3 = cuePos.toF3()
        val objF3 = objPos.toF3()

        val topRailZ = ARConstants.TABLE_DEPTH / 2.0f
        val bottomRailZ = -ARConstants.TABLE_DEPTH / 2.0f
        val rightRailX = ARConstants.TABLE_WIDTH / 2.0f
        val leftRailX = -ARConstants.TABLE_WIDTH / 2.0f

        val mirroredObjPos: Float3
        val railAimPoint: Float3

        when (selectedRail) {
            Rail.TOP -> {
                mirroredObjPos = Float3(objF3.x, objF3.y, topRailZ + (topRailZ - objF3.z))
                val t = (topRailZ - cueF3.z) / (mirroredObjPos.z - cueF3.z)
                railAimPoint = cueF3 + t * (mirroredObjPos - cueF3)
            }
            Rail.BOTTOM -> {
                mirroredObjPos = Float3(objF3.x, objF3.y, bottomRailZ + (bottomRailZ - objF3.z))
                val t = (bottomRailZ - cueF3.z) / (mirroredObjPos.z - cueF3.z)
                railAimPoint = cueF3 + t * (mirroredObjPos - cueF3)
            }
            Rail.RIGHT -> {
                mirroredObjPos = Float3(rightRailX + (rightRailX - objF3.x), objF3.y, objF3.z)
                val t = (rightRailX - cueF3.x) / (mirroredObjPos.x - cueF3.x)
                railAimPoint = cueF3 + t * (mirroredObjPos - cueF3)
            }
            Rail.LEFT -> {
                mirroredObjPos = Float3(leftRailX + (leftRailX - objF3.x), objF3.y, objF3.z)
                val t = (leftRailX - cueF3.x) / (mirroredObjPos.x - cueF3.x)
                railAimPoint = cueF3 + t * (mirroredObjPos - cueF3)
            }
        }

        anchorNode.addChild(LineNode(scope, cueF3, railAimPoint, AccentGold))
        anchorNode.addChild(LineNode(scope, railAimPoint, objF3, RustedEmber))

        val incomingVec = (railAimPoint - cueF3).normalize()
        val outgoingVec = (objF3 - railAimPoint).normalize()
        val bankAngle = angleBetween(incomingVec, outgoingVec)
        val angleText = "%.1f°".format(bankAngle)
        anchorNode.addChild(TextNode(scope, context, angleText))
            .apply { position = railAimPoint + Position(y = 0.1f) }
    }

    fun drawSpinIndicator(anchorNode: AnchorNode, scope: CoroutineScope, cuePos: Position?, spinOffset: Offset) {
        if (cuePos == null || spinOffset == Offset.Zero) return

        val cueBallNode = anchorNode.children.firstOrNull { it is BallNode && distance(it.worldPosition, cuePos) < 0.01f }
        if (cueBallNode != null) {
            val indicatorRadius = 0.005f
            val ballRadius = ARConstants.BALL_DIAMETER / 2f
            val indicatorPosition = Position(
                x = spinOffset.x * (ballRadius - indicatorRadius),
                y = -spinOffset.y * (ballRadius - indicatorRadius), // Y on screen is inverted on the ball
                z = ballRadius // Place it on the front surface of the ball
            )

            val indicatorNode = SpinIndicatorNode(scope, WarningRed, radius = indicatorRadius)
            indicatorNode.position = indicatorPosition
            // Orient the indicator to face away from the ball's center, along the Z axis initially
            indicatorNode.lookAt(Position(0f, 0f, 1f))
            cueBallNode.addChild(indicatorNode)
        }
    }

    private fun distance(p1: Position, p2: Position): Float {
        return sqrt((p1.x - p2.x).pow(2) + (p1.y - p2.y).pow(2) + (p1.z - p2.z).pow(2))
    }
}


--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ar/BallNode.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar

import com.google.ar.sceneform.rendering.MaterialFactory
import com.google.ar.sceneform.rendering.ShapeFactory
import dev.romainguy.kotlin.math.Float3
import io.github.sceneview.material.setBaseColor
import io.github.sceneview.math.toOldColor
import io.github.sceneview.node.Node
import kotlinx.coroutines.CoroutineScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class BallNode(
    coroutineScope: CoroutineScope,
    color: androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color,
    radius: Float = 0.028575f // Standard pool ball radius in meters
) : Node() {
    init {
        coroutineScope.launch {
            val material = MaterialFactory.makeOpaqueWithColor(engine, color.toOldColor()).await()
            val renderable = ShapeFactory.makeSphere(engine,
                radius = radius,
                center = Float3(x = 0.0f, y = radius, z = 0.0f), // Center sphere on its bottom point
                material = material
            )
            setRenderable(renderable)
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ar/LineNode.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar

import com.google.ar.sceneform.rendering.MaterialFactory
import com.google.ar.sceneform.rendering.ShapeFactory
import dev.romainguy.kotlin.math.Float3
import io.github.sceneview.math.toNewQuaternion
import io.github.sceneview.math.toNewVector3
import io.github.sceneview.math.toOldColor
import io.github.sceneview.math.toOldQuaternion
import io.github.sceneview.math.toOldVector3
import io.github.sceneview.node.Node
import io.github.sceneview.utils.lookAt
import kotlinx.coroutines.CoroutineScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class LineNode(
    coroutineScope: CoroutineScope,
    start: Float3,
    end: Float3,
    color: androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color,
    radius: Float = 0.002f
) : Node() {

    init {
        coroutineScope.launch {
            val material = MaterialFactory.makeOpaqueWithColor(engine, color.toOldColor()).await()

            val difference = end - start
            val directionFromTopToBottom = difference.normalize()
            val rotation = lookAt(directionFromTopToBottom, Float3(y = 1.0f)).toOldQuaternion()

            val renderable = ShapeFactory.makeCylinder(
                engine,
                radius,
                difference.length,
                Float3(),
                material
            )

            setRenderable(renderable)

            // Position the line at its center
            position = (start + end) / 2.0f
            // Rotate the line to point from start to end
            this.rotation = rotation.toNewQuaternion()
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ar/MathUtils.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar

import dev.romainguy.kotlin.math.Float3
import dev.romainguy.kotlin.math.dot
import io.github.sceneview.math.Position
import kotlin.math.acos
import kotlin.math.pow
import kotlin.math.sqrt

object MathUtils {
    fun Position.toF3() = Float3(this.x, this.y, this.z)
    fun Float3.toPosition() = Position(this.x, this.y, this.z)

    fun Float3.length(): Float = sqrt(this.x.pow(2) + this.y.pow(2) + this.z.pow(2))
    fun Float3.normalize(): Float3 {
        val len = length()
        return if (len > 0) this / len else this
    }

    /**
     * Calculates the angle in degrees between two vectors.
     */
    fun angleBetween(vec1: Float3, vec2: Float3): Float {
        val dotProduct = dot(vec1.normalize(), vec2.normalize())
        // Clamp the dot product to avoid NaN from acos due to floating point inaccuracies
        val clampedDot = dotProduct.coerceIn(-1.0f, 1.0f)
        return Math.toDegrees(acos(clampedDot).toDouble()).toFloat()
    }
}


--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ar/SpinIndicatorNode.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar

import androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color
import com.google.ar.sceneform.rendering.MaterialFactory
import com.google.ar.sceneform.rendering.ShapeFactory
import dev.romainguy.kotlin.math.Float3
import io.github.sceneview.math.toOldColor
import io.github.sceneview.node.Node
import kotlinx.coroutines.CoroutineScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class SpinIndicatorNode(
    coroutineScope: CoroutineScope,
    color: Color,
    radius: Float = 0.005f // Small dot
) : Node() {
    init {
        coroutineScope.launch {
            val material = MaterialFactory.makeOpaqueWithColor(engine, color.toOldColor()).await()
            val renderable = ShapeFactory.makeCylinder(engine,
                radius = radius,
                height = 0.001f, // Almost flat
                center = Float3(),
                material = material
            )
            setRenderable(renderable)
            // Rotate it to be flat
            rotation = Float3(x = 90.0f, y = 0.0f, z = 0.0f)
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ar/TableNode.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar

import com.google.ar.sceneform.rendering.MaterialFactory
import com.google.ar.sceneform.rendering.ShapeFactory
import dev.romainguy.kotlin.math.Float3
import io.github.sceneview.math.toOldColor
import io.github.sceneview.node.Node
import kotlinx.coroutines.CoroutineScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class TableNode(
    coroutineScope: CoroutineScope,
    tableWidth: Float,
    tableDepth: Float,
) : Node() {

    companion object {
        private val BED_COLOR = androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color(0.0f, 0.4f, 0.15f, 1.0f)
        private val RAIL_COLOR = androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color(0.35f, 0.2f, 0.05f, 1.0f)
    }

    val bedNode: Node = Node(engine)

    init {
        // This parent node is the anchor point. We add children to it.
        name = "TableGroup"
        bedNode.name = "TableBed"
        addChild(bedNode)

        coroutineScope.launch {
            // Create materials for the bed and rails
            val bedMaterial = MaterialFactory.makeOpaqueWithColor(engine, BED_COLOR.toOldColor()).await()
            val railMaterial = MaterialFactory.makeOpaqueWithColor(engine, RAIL_COLOR.toOldColor()).await()

            // 1. Create the table bed (playing surface) and attach it to the bedNode
            val bedRenderable = ShapeFactory.makeCube(engine,
                size = Float3(x = tableWidth, y = 0.01f, z = tableDepth),
                center = Float3(x = 0.0f, y = -0.005f, z = 0.0f), // Center on its top surface
                material = bedMaterial
            )
            bedNode.setRenderable(bedRenderable)

            // 2. Create the rails and attach them to the MAIN TableNode (this)
            // This way, they rotate with the table but are conceptually separate from the bed for hit testing.
            val halfDepth = tableDepth / 2.0f
            val halfWidth = tableWidth / 2.0f
            val railYPos = ARConstants.RAIL_HEIGHT / 2.0f

            // Top Rail
            val topRail = Node(engine).apply {
                val renderable = ShapeFactory.makeCube(engine,
                    size = Float3(x = tableWidth + (2 * ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH), y = ARConstants.RAIL_HEIGHT, z = ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH),
                    center = Float3(x = 0f, y = railYPos, z = 0f),
                    material = railMaterial
                )
                setRenderable(renderable)
                position = Float3(x = 0f, y = 0f, z = -halfDepth - (ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH / 2.0f))
            }
            addChild(topRail)

            // Bottom Rail
            val bottomRail = Node(engine).apply {
                val renderable = ShapeFactory.makeCube(engine,
                    size = Float3(x = tableWidth + (2 * ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH), y = ARConstants.RAIL_HEIGHT, z = ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH),
                    center = Float3(x = 0f, y = railYPos, z = 0f),
                    material = railMaterial
                )
                setRenderable(renderable)
                position = Float3(x = 0f, y = 0f, z = halfDepth + (ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH / 2.0f))
            }
            addChild(bottomRail)

            // Left Rail
            val leftRail = Node(engine).apply {
                val renderable = ShapeFactory.makeCube(engine,
                    size = Float3(x = ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH, y = ARConstants.RAIL_HEIGHT, z = tableDepth),
                    center = Float3(x = 0f, y = railYPos, z = 0f),
                    material = railMaterial
                )
                setRenderable(renderable)
                position = Float3(x = -halfWidth - (ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH / 2.0f), y = 0f, z = 0f)
            }
            addChild(leftRail)

            // Right Rail
            val rightRail = Node(engine).apply {
                val renderable = ShapeFactory.makeCube(engine,
                    size = Float3(x = ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH, y = ARConstants.RAIL_HEIGHT, z = tableDepth),
                    center = Float3(x = 0f, y = railYPos, z = 0f),
                    material = railMaterial
                )
                setRenderable(renderable)
                position = Float3(x = halfWidth + (ARConstants.RAIL_WIDTH / 2.0f), y = 0f, z = 0f)
            }
            addChild(rightRail)
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ar/TextNode.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar

import android.content.Context
import android.view.Gravity
import android.widget.TextView
import androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color
import com.google.ar.sceneform.rendering.ViewRenderable
import io.github.sceneview.math.Position
import io.github.sceneview.math.toOldColor
import io.github.sceneview.node.Node
import kotlinx.coroutines.CoroutineScope
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch

class TextNode(
    coroutineScope: CoroutineScope,
    context: Context,
    text: String,
    textColor: Color = Color.White,
    backgroundColor: Color = Color.Black.copy(alpha = 0.5f)
) : Node() {
    init {
        coroutineScope.launch {
            val renderable = ViewRenderable.builder()
                .setView(context, TextView(context).apply {
                    this.text = text
                    this.setTextColor(textColor.toOldColor().toArgb())
                    this.setBackgroundColor(backgroundColor.toOldColor().toArgb())
                    this.gravity = Gravity.CENTER
                    this.textSize = 18f // sp
                    setPadding(32, 8, 32, 8)
                }).build().await()
            setRenderable(renderable)

            // Make it always face the camera
            isForwardFacing = true
        }
    }
}

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.di

import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.network.GithubApi
import dagger.Module
import dagger.Provides
import dagger.hilt.InstallIn
import dagger.hilt.components.SingletonComponent
import retrofit2.Retrofit
import retrofit2.converter.gson.GsonConverterFactory
import javax.inject.Singleton

@Module
@InstallIn(SingletonComponent::class)
object AppModule {

    @Provides
    @Singleton
    fun provideGithubApi(): GithubApi {
        return Retrofit.Builder()
            .baseUrl("https://api.github.com/")
            .addConverterFactory(GsonConverterFactory.create())
            .build()
            .create(GithubApi::class.java)
    }
}

--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ui/MainScreen.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui

import android.view.MotionEvent
import androidx.compose.foundation.background
import androidx.compose.foundation.layout.*
import androidx.compose.material.icons.Icons
import androidx.compose.material.icons.filled.Refresh
import androidx.compose.material3.*
import androidx.compose.runtime.*
import androidx.compose.ui.Alignment
import androidx.compose.ui.Modifier
import androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color
import androidx.compose.ui.platform.LocalContext
import androidx.compose.ui.res.painterResource
import androidx.compose.ui.text.style.TextAlign
import androidx.compose.ui.unit.dp
import androidx.hilt.navigation.compose.hiltViewModel
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.R
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ar.*
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui.composables.SpinControl
import io.github.sceneview.ar.ARScene
import io.github.sceneview.ar.arcore.getUpdatedPlanes
import io.github.sceneview.ar.node.AnchorNode
import io.github.sceneview.ar.rememberARCameraNode
import io.github.sceneview.math.Position
import io.github.sceneview.math.Rotation

@OptIn(ExperimentalMaterial3Api::class)
@Composable
fun MainScreen(viewModel: MainViewModel = hiltViewModel()) {
    val uiState by viewModel.uiState.collectAsState()
    val coroutineScope = rememberCoroutineScope()
    var arSceneView by remember { mutableStateOf<ARScene?>(null) }
    val cameraNode = rememberARCameraNode()
    val context = LocalContext.current

    Scaffold(
        topBar = {
            CenterAlignedTopAppBar(
                title = { Text(uiState.statusText, textAlign = TextAlign.Center) },
                colors = TopAppBarDefaults.centerAlignedTopAppBarColors(containerColor = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.surface.copy(alpha = 0.7f))
            )
        },
        floatingActionButton = {
            Column(horizontalAlignment = Alignment.End, verticalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(12.dp)) {
                if (uiState.appState > AppState.DetectingPlane) {
                    FloatingActionButton(onClick = { viewModel.reset() }) {
                        Icon(Icons.Default.Refresh, contentDescription = "Reset Scene")
                    }
                }
                if (uiState.appState >= AppState.TablePlaced) {
                    FloatingActionButton(
                        onClick = { viewModel.toggleBankingMode() },
                        containerColor = if (uiState.isBankingMode) MaterialTheme.colorScheme.tertiaryContainer else MaterialTheme.colorScheme.secondaryContainer
                    ) {
                        Icon(painter = painterResource(id = R.drawable.ic_banking_mode), contentDescription = "Toggle Banking Mode")
                    }
                }
            }
        },
        floatingActionButtonPosition = FabPosition.End,
        content = { paddingValues ->
            Box(modifier = Modifier.padding(paddingValues).fillMaxSize()) {
                ARScene(
                    modifier = Modifier.fillMaxSize(),
                    nodes = if (uiState.tableAnchorNode != null) listOfNotNull(uiState.tableAnchorNode) else emptyList(),
                    planeRenderer = true, cameraNode = cameraNode,
                    onSessionUpdated = { _, frame ->
                        if (uiState.appState == AppState.DetectingPlane && frame.getUpdatedPlanes().isNotEmpty()) {
                            viewModel.onPlaneDetected(true)
                        }
                    },
                    onTap = { motionEvent, hitResult ->
                        if (motionEvent.action == MotionEvent.ACTION_DOWN && uiState.appState >= AppState.TablePlaced && hitResult != null) {
                            val tableBedNode = uiState.tableAnchorNode?.children?.filterIsInstance<TableNode>()?.firstOrNull()?.bedNode
                            if (hitResult.node == tableBedNode) {
                                viewModel.onBallPlaced(Position(hitResult.hitPose.translation))
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    onViewCreated = { arScene -> arSceneView = arScene }
                )

                if (uiState.appState == AppState.PlaneDetected) {
                    Box(modifier = Modifier.fillMaxSize(), contentAlignment = Alignment.Center) {
                        Button(onClick = {
                            arSceneView?.let { scene ->
                                scene.createAnchorOrNull(scene.camera.pose)?.let { anchor ->
                                    val anchorNode = AnchorNode(engine = scene.engine, anchor = anchor)
                                    viewModel.onTablePlaced(anchorNode)
                                }
                            }
                        }) { Text("Place Table") }
                    }
                }

                // Bottom Controls
                Column(modifier = Modifier.align(Alignment.BottomCenter).padding(bottom = 16.dp).fillMaxWidth(), horizontalAlignment = Alignment.CenterHorizontally) {
                    if (uiState.isBankingMode) {
                        RailSelectionControls(selectedRail = uiState.selectedRail, onRailSelected = { viewModel.selectRail(it) })
                        Spacer(Modifier.height(8.dp))
                        Slider(value = uiState.tableRotationDegrees, onValueChange = { viewModel.updateTableRotation(it) }, valueRange = 0f..179f, modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(0.9f))
                    } else if (uiState.appState == AppState.ObjectBallSet) {
                        SpinControl(onSpinChanged = { viewModel.onSpinChanged(it) })
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    )

    LaunchedEffect(uiState) {
        val anchorNode = uiState.tableAnchorNode ?: return@LaunchedEffect
        val cuePos = uiState.cueBallPosition
        val objPos = uiState.objectBallPosition

        val tableNode = anchorNode.children.filterIsInstance<TableNode>().firstOrNull() ?: run {
            TableNode(coroutineScope, ARConstants.TABLE_WIDTH, ARConstants.TABLE_DEPTH).also { anchorNode.addChild(it) }
        }
        tableNode.rotation = Rotation(0f, uiState.tableRotationDegrees, 0f)

        anchorNode.children.filterNot { it is TableNode }.forEach { it.destroy() }

        if (cuePos != null) {
            anchorNode.addChild(BallNode(coroutineScope, Color.White).apply { position = cuePos })
            ARViewRenderer.drawSpinIndicator(anchorNode, coroutineScope, cuePos, uiState.spinOffset)
        }
        if (objPos != null) {
            anchorNode.addChild(BallNode(coroutineScope, Color.Yellow).apply { position = objPos })
        }

        if (cuePos != null && objPos != null) {
            if (uiState.isBankingMode) {
                ARViewRenderer.drawBankShotLines(anchorNode, coroutineScope, context, cuePos, objPos, uiState.selectedRail)
            } else {
                ARViewRenderer.drawCutShotLines(anchorNode, coroutineScope, context, cuePos, objPos, uiState.spinOffset)
            }
        }
    }
}

@Composable
fun RailSelectionControls(selectedRail: Rail, onRailSelected: (Rail) -> Unit) {
    Card(colors = CardDefaults.cardColors(containerColor = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.surface.copy(alpha = 0.7f))) {
        Row(
            modifier = Modifier.padding(vertical = 4.dp, horizontal = 8.dp),
            horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(8.dp),
            verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically
        ) {
            Icon(painter = painterResource(id = R.drawable.ic_rail_select), contentDescription = "Select Rail")
            Rail.entries.forEach { rail ->
                val isSelected = selectedRail == rail
                OutlinedButton(
                    onClick = { onRailSelected(rail) },
                    colors = ButtonDefaults.outlinedButtonColors(containerColor = if (isSelected) MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary else Color.Transparent),
                    contentPadding = PaddingValues(horizontal = 12.dp, vertical = 4.dp)
                ) {
                    Text(rail.name.first().toString(), color = if (isSelected) MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onPrimary else MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurface)
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

// app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ui/MainScreenEvent.kt
package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui

import android.graphics.PointF
import androidx.compose.material3.ColorScheme
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.data.FullOrientation
import com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.view.state.ToastMessage

sealed class MainScreenEvent {
    data class SizeChanged(val width: Int, val height: Int) : MainScreenEvent()
    data class ZoomSliderChanged(val position: Float) : MainScreenEvent()
    data class ZoomScaleChanged(val scaleFactor: Float) : MainScreenEvent()

    // Protractor System Events
    data class RotationChanged(val newRotation: Float) : MainScreenEvent()
    data class UnitMoved(val position: PointF) : MainScreenEvent() // This is screen point

    // ActualCueBall / BankingBall Events
    data class ActualCueBallMoved(val position: PointF) : MainScreenEvent() // This is screen point

    // Banking System Events
    data class TableRotationChanged(val degrees: Float) : MainScreenEvent()
    data class BankingAimTargetDragged(val screenPoint: PointF) : MainScreenEvent() // This is screen point, ViewModel will convert to logical

    internal data class UpdateLogicalActualCueBallPosition(val logicalPoint: PointF) : MainScreenEvent()
    internal data class UpdateLogicalUnitPosition(val logicalPoint: PointF) : MainScreenEvent()
    internal data class UpdateLogicalBankingAimTarget(val logicalPoint: PointF) : MainScreenEvent()

    data class FullOrientationChanged(val orientation: FullOrientation) : MainScreenEvent()

    data class ThemeChanged(val scheme: ColorScheme) : MainScreenEvent()

    object ToggleForceTheme : MainScreenEvent()
    object ToggleLuminanceDialog : MainScreenEvent()
    data class AdjustLuminance(val adjustment: Float) : MainScreenEvent()

    data class ShowToast(val message: ToastMessage) : MainScreenEvent()

    object StartTutorial : MainScreenEvent()
    object NextTutorialStep : MainScreenEvent()
    object EndTutorial : MainScreenEvent()

    object Reset : MainScreenEvent()
    object ToggleHelp : MainScreenEvent()
    object ToggleActualCueBall : MainScreenEvent()
    object ToggleBankingMode : MainScreenEvent()

    data class ToggleSpatialLock(val isLocked: Boolean) : MainScreenEvent()

    object CheckForUpdate : MainScreenEvent()
    object ViewArt : MainScreenEvent()
    object FeatureComingSoon : MainScreenEvent()
    object ShowDonationOptions : MainScreenEvent()
    object SingleEventConsumed : MainScreenEvent()
    object ToastShown : MainScreenEvent()
    object GestureStarted : MainScreenEvent()
    object GestureEnded : MainScreenEvent()
}


--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ui/MainViewModel.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui

import androidx.compose.ui.geometry.Offset
import androidx.lifecycle.ViewModel
import androidx.lifecycle.viewModelScope
import dagger.hilt.android.lifecycle.HiltViewModel
import io.github.sceneview.ar.node.AnchorNode
import io.github.sceneview.math.Position
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.MutableStateFlow
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.asStateFlow
import kotlinx.coroutines.flow.update
import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
import javax.inject.Inject

enum class AppState {
    DetectingPlane,
    PlaneDetected,
    TablePlaced,
    CueBallSet,
    ObjectBallSet
}

enum class Rail { TOP, BOTTOM, LEFT, RIGHT }

data class CueVisionUiState(
    val appState: AppState = AppState.DetectingPlane,
    val statusText: String = "Move your phone to detect a surface",
    val tableAnchorNode: AnchorNode? = null,
    val cueBallPosition: Position? = null,
    val objectBallPosition: Position? = null,
    val isBankingMode: Boolean = false,
    val tableRotationDegrees: Float = 0f,
    val selectedRail: Rail = Rail.TOP,
    val spinOffset: Offset = Offset.Zero
)

@HiltViewModel
class MainViewModel @Inject constructor() : ViewModel() {

    private val _uiState = MutableStateFlow(CueVisionUiState())
    val uiState = _uiState.asStateFlow()

    fun onPlaneDetected(hasPlanes: Boolean) {
        if (uiState.value.appState == AppState.DetectingPlane && hasPlanes) {
            _uiState.update { it.copy(appState = AppState.PlaneDetected, statusText = getStatusText(AppState.PlaneDetected)) }
        }
    }

    fun onTablePlaced(anchorNode: AnchorNode) {
        _uiState.update {
            it.copy(
                appState = AppState.TablePlaced,
                statusText = getStatusText(AppState.TablePlaced),
                tableAnchorNode = anchorNode
            )
        }
    }

    fun onBallPlaced(position: Position) {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            when (uiState.value.appState) {
                AppState.TablePlaced, AppState.CueBallSet -> {
                    if (uiState.value.cueBallPosition == null) {
                        _uiState.update {
                            it.copy(
                                appState = AppState.CueBallSet,
                                statusText = getStatusText(AppState.CueBallSet),
                                cueBallPosition = position
                            )
                        }
                    } else {
                        _uiState.update {
                            it.copy(
                                appState = AppState.ObjectBallSet,
                                statusText = getStatusText(AppState.ObjectBallSet, it.isBankingMode),
                                objectBallPosition = position
                            )
                        }
                    }
                }
                // Allow repositioning by re-tapping
                AppState.ObjectBallSet -> {
                    _uiState.update {
                        it.copy(
                            appState = AppState.CueBallSet, // Go back to setting object ball
                            statusText = "Cue ball set. Tap to place a new Object Ball.",
                            objectBallPosition = null, // Clear object ball to place a new one
                            cueBallPosition = position // The new tap sets the cue ball
                        )
                    }
                }
                else -> {}
            }
        }
    }

    fun onSpinChanged(offset: Offset) {
        _uiState.update { it.copy(spinOffset = offset) }
    }

    fun toggleBankingMode() {
        val isNowBanking = !uiState.value.isBankingMode
        _uiState.update {
            it.copy(
                isBankingMode = isNowBanking,
                statusText = getStatusText(it.appState, isNowBanking)
            )
        }
    }

    fun updateTableRotation(degrees: Float) {
        if (uiState.value.isBankingMode) {
            _uiState.update { it.copy(tableRotationDegrees = degrees) }
        }
    }

    fun selectRail(rail: Rail) {
        _uiState.update { it.copy(selectedRail = rail) }
    }

    fun reset() {
        uiState.value.tableAnchorNode?.destroy()
        _uiState.value = CueVisionUiState()
    }

    private fun getStatusText(appState: AppState, isBankingMode: Boolean = false): String {
        return when (appState) {
            AppState.DetectingPlane -> "Move your phone to detect a surface"
            AppState.PlaneDetected -> "Surface detected. Tap button to place table."
            AppState.TablePlaced -> "Table placed. Tap on the table to place the Cue Ball."
            AppState.CueBallSet -> "Cue ball set. Tap to place an Object Ball."
            AppState.ObjectBallSet -> if (isBankingMode) "Bank Mode. Use controls to adjust." else "Cut Shot Mode. Use spin control."
        }
    }
}

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui

/**
 * A sealed class to represent all possible user actions originating from UI menus or buttons.
 * This provides a clean, type-safe way to pass events from the UI to the ViewModel.
 */
sealed class MenuAction {
    object Reset : MenuAction()
    object ToggleHelp : MenuAction()
    object ToggleJumpingBall : MenuAction()
    object CheckForUpdate : MenuAction()
    object ToggleTheme : MenuAction()
}


--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ui/theme/Color.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui.theme

import androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color

val AccentGold = Color(0xFFBDA559)

val AshlineFog = Color(0xFFBFBFBF)      // High-vis neutral
val RebelYellow = Color(0xFFFFD000)  // Primary yellow
val BurntBrass = Color(0xFF8A5A00)   // Dirty metallic accent
val SmokeyGrunge = Color(0xFF3B3B3B) // Deep, gritty gray (but not black)


val TargetGold = Color(0xFFFFB700)   // Vibrant highlight gold
val MellowYellow = Color(0xFFD4AF37)    // Muted gold
val AgedAmber = Color(0xFFC69026)       // Secondary accent

--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ui/theme/Theme.kt ---

package com.hereliesaz.cuedetat.ui.theme

import android.app.Activity
import androidx.compose.material3.MaterialTheme
import androidx.compose.material3.darkColorScheme
import androidx.compose.runtime.Composable
import androidx.compose.runtime.SideEffect
import androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color
import androidx.compose.ui.graphics.toArgb
import androidx.compose.ui.platform.LocalView
import androidx.core.view.WindowCompat

private val DarkColorScheme = darkColorScheme(
    primary = AccentGold,
    secondary = AcidPatina,
    tertiary = MutedMaroon,
    background = Color(0xFF121212),
    surface = Color(0xFF1E1E1E),
    surfaceVariant = Color(0xFF2C2C2E),
    onPrimary = Color.Black,
    onSecondary = Color.Black,
    onTertiary = Color.White,
    onBackground = Color(0xFFE0E0E0),
    onSurface = Color(0xFFE0E0E0),
    onSurfaceVariant = Color(0xFFCFCFCF),
    error = WarningRed
)

@Composable
fun CueDetatARTheme(
    content: @Composable () -> Unit
) {
    val colorScheme = DarkColorScheme
    val view = LocalView.current
    if (!view.isInEditMode) {
        SideEffect {
            val window = (view.context as Activity).window
            window.statusBarColor = Color.Transparent.toArgb()
            window.navigationBarColor = Color.Transparent.toArgb()
            WindowCompat.getInsetsController(window, view).isAppearanceLightStatusBars = false
        }
    }

    MaterialTheme(
        colorScheme = colorScheme,
        typography = Typography,
        shapes = Shapes,
        content = content
    )
}--- FILE: app/src/main/java/com/hereliesaz/cuedetat/ui/theme/Type.kt ---
